## ┬د2 Agent_factor ظ¤ activation & validation history

> Extracted verbatim from sprint-workflow.md ┬دStep 1 ┬دActive Agent Delegation Factor Modifier (activation evidence + tier-2/3/4 split evolution + per-sprint activation/validation history Sprint 57.42 to 57.62 + deprecated baselines). The lean active rules (Formula tier-4 table + Rollback + Escalation + Tracking) live in sprint-workflow.md.

#### Active Agent Delegation Factor Modifier (ACTIVATED 2026-05-25 ظ¤ Sprint 57.42 retro structural decision per `AD-Sprint-Plan-Agent-Delegation-Factor-Modifier`)

**Status**: **ACTIVE ظ¤ Option A multiplicative `agent_factor` coefficient with mid-band start `0.55`**. Closes `AD-Sprint-Plan-Agent-Delegation-Factor-Modifier`. Activation criteria FULLY MET at Sprint 57.42 retro Q4 (5 cross-class data points + 4 consecutive `mockup-strict-rebuild` agent-delegated < 0.7).

**Hypothesis (validated)**: code-implementer agent-delegated frontend work shows ~3-5├ù speedup vs the human-rewrite cadence the bottom-up estimates assume. Existing per-class multipliers (0.45-0.85) bake in a human-cadence haircut; agent-delegated sprints consistently undershoot the calibrated band lower edge because the haircut isn't enough. Validated by 5 data points below.

**Activation evidence** (5 data points across 2 classes):

| Sprint / FIX | Class | Delegation | Ratio actual/committed | Ratio actual/bottom-up | Implied agent vs human speedup |
|--------------|-------|------------|------------------------|------------------------|--------------------------------|
| Sprint 57.39 | `-with-extras` (0.65) | 6th+7th consecutive code-implementer (4-domain batched) | **0.41** ظô band -0.44 | 0.27 | ~3.7├ù |
| FIX-015 (post-hoc) | bundled FIX (no class) | code-implementer 6 child re-point | n/a (no class) | **~0.04** | ~24-40├ù (outlier ظ¤ surgical token-swap) |
| Sprint 57.40 | `frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild` (0.60) | 7th consecutive code-implementer | **0.36** ظô band -0.49 | 0.21 | ~4.7├ù |
| Sprint 57.41 | `frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild` (0.60) | 8th+9th consecutive code-implementer | **0.18** ظô band -0.67 | 0.10 | ~10├ù (Day 2 ~3.4 min outlier) |
| Sprint 57.42 | `frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild` (0.60) | 10th+11th consecutive code-implementer | **0.33** ظô band -0.52 | 0.20 | ~5├ù |

4-consecutive `mockup-strict-rebuild` agent-delegated mean **~0.29** (excluding 57.39 cross-class point).

**Formula** (applies from Sprint 57.43+ onwards):

```
effective_calibrated_hours = bottom_up ├ù scope_class_multiplier ├ù agent_factor

where agent_factor = {
  human (default):      1.0
  agent-delegated (tier-4 sub-class table ظ¤ Sprint 57.55 retro Q4 tier-4 SPLIT ACTIVATED effective 2026-05-28 onwards):
    mechanical-pattern-reuse-heavy:               0.30   (ظëح 4 mechanical repetitions of same template in 1 sprint; evidence: Sprint 57.49 retroactive ظ¤ 5-tab+1-drawer migration ratio 0.21 under 0.30 vs 0.14 under 0.45; Sprint 57.60 1st DELIBERATE FORWARD application ratio ~1.09 IN BAND ظ£à ظ¤ backend 5-site fallback removal + 0020 cleanup migration + test conversions; KEEP 0.30 single forward-data-point; counterfactual `-port-style` 0.45 ظْ ~0.73 below band so 0.30 better fit; shape-variance: 57.49 high-repetition ~24├ù ratio 0.21 vs 57.60 moderate-repetition ratio 1.09 ظ¤ if a future ظëح20├ù sprint at 0.30 lands < 0.7 again consider tier refinement `-high-repetition` ~0.20 vs `-moderate` 0.30, defer until 2+ such data points)
    mechanical-greenfield-port-style:             0.45   (single NEW component-pair via mirror-port of existing service shape; predecessor template ظëح 95% internalized; NO NEW Pydantic schema design / UX state design ظ¤ RESERVED for future port-only sprints)
    mechanical-greenfield-design-decisions:       0.65   (single NEW component-pair WITH NEW Pydantic schema design + NEW UX state design ظ¤ e.g. edit-mode draft state ظ¤ design decisions add ~30-50% wall-clock vs pure port; evidence: Sprint 57.54 HITLPolicies WRITE ratio ~1.37-2.0 at 0.50 / Sprint 57.55 FeatureFlags WRITE ratio ~1.57 at 0.50 ظ¤ 2 consec > 1.20 ظْ tier-4 SPLIT ACTIVATED; equivalent ratios under 0.65 = 1.05-1.55 / 1.21 ظْ band top edge / IN band; Sprint 57.56=1.02 + 57.57=1.15 both IN band 2-consec ظْ SPLIT FULLY VALIDATED; **Sprint 57.61 3rd validation 1st BACKEND-ONLY ratio ~0.74 BELOW band by 0.11** ظ¤ single BELOW point vs 2 IN ظْ rollback rule needs 2 consec same-direction ظْ KEEP 0.65 single-data-point caution; backend-only validator+422-envelope runs faster than the backend+frontend pair the 0.65 was calibrated on, counterfactual `-port-style` 0.45 ظْ ~1.06 IN band ظْ NEW carryover `AD-AgentFactor-DesignDecisions-BackendOnly-Variant-Watch` needs 2nd backend-only point before any sub-class refinement; **Sprint 57.62 4th validation BACK TO PAIR SHAPE ratio ~0.77 BELOW band by 0.08** ظ¤ pair sub-seq 57.56=1.02 + 57.57=1.15 + 57.62=0.77 mean ~0.98 IN band ظْ KEEP 0.65 single-data-point-per-shape; **R6 WEAKENS** ظ¤ 57.61 backend-only 0.74 + 57.62 pair 0.77 = 2 consec below regardless of shape ظْ likely agent over-delivers generally; `AD-AgentFactor-DesignDecisions-Below-Band-Watch` broadens cross-shape: next `-design-decisions` (either shape) < 0.85 ظْ tighten 0.65 ظْ 0.55)
    mixed-multidomain-bundle-mechanical:          0.45   (3+ independent tracks WITH mechanical pattern reuse component ظ¤ e.g. backend ORM + Pydantic + tests bundle; History: Sprint 57.46 ratio 1.60 at 0.45ظْrollback 0.65 (Option B); Sprint 57.58 tier-3 1st validation ~0.49 BELOW band single-data-point KEEP 0.65; Sprint 57.59 tier-3 2nd validation ~0.34 BELOW band ظْ 2 consec < 0.7 ROLLBACK RULE MET ظْ **tighten 0.65 ظْ 0.45 effective Sprint 57.60+**; note even 0.45 ظëê 0.49 still below band ظ¤ if Sprint 57.60 1st validation under 0.45 also < 0.7 ظْ escalate 0.30 OR fold into mechanical-pattern-reuse-heavy 0.30)
    mixed-multidomain-bundle-non-mechanical:      1.0    (3+ independent tracks of pure audit/docs/rules ظ¤ NO mechanical pattern reuse; e.g. Sprint 57.51 + 57.52 both ratios > 1.20 at 0.65 = 2nd rollback-trigger MET; tier-3 SPLIT Sprint 57.52 retro effective 2026-05-27 onwards)
  partial (20-79% via agent):          0.75   (linear interpolation)
  human (<20% via agent):              1.0
  History: 0.55 (Sprint 57.42 activated) ظْ 0.45 (Sprint 57.44 tighten) ظْ 0.65 (Sprint 57.46 rollback) ظْ Option B sub-class split (Sprint 57.48; mechanical-single-domain 0.45 + mixed-multidomain-bundle 0.65) ظْ Option B tier-2 split (Sprint 57.50; closes AD-AgentFactor-Tier-2-Refinement-Proposal; mechanical-single-domain split into pattern-reuse-heavy 0.30 + greenfield 0.50; parallel Sprint 57.38 `-simple/-with-extras` precedent + Sprint 57.48 Option B precedent) ظْ Option B tier-3 split (Sprint 57.52; mixed-multidomain-bundle split into -mechanical 0.65 unchanged + -non-mechanical 1.0 NEW; closes AD-AgentFactor-Tier-2-MixedBundle-Validation-Sprint-57.52; rollback rule "2 sprints with ratio > 1.20 ظْ mandatory structural action" MET via Sprint 57.51=1.49 + Sprint 57.52=~1.85) ظْ Option B tier-4 split (Sprint 57.55; mechanical-greenfield split into -port-style 0.45 RESERVED + -design-decisions 0.65 NEW; closes AD-Sub-Class-Greenfield-Port-vs-Design-Refinement Sprint 57.54 CONDITIONAL carryover; rollback rule MET via Sprint 57.54 ratio ~1.37-2.0 + Sprint 57.55 ratio ~1.57 ظ¤ both > 1.20 at 0.50 baseline)
}
```

**When `agent-delegated` applies**: ظëح 80% of Day 1 work via code-implementer agent (or equivalent). 20-79% = `partial` (apply `agent_factor = 0.75` linear interpolation; record explicit tag in retro Q2). < 20% = `human` (apply `agent_factor = 1.0`; existing class multiplier alone).

**Equivalent combined ratios under `agent_factor = 0.45`** (tightened 2026-05-26):

| Class | Base mult | ├ù 0.45 | Predicted band hit (vs historical actuals at prior 0.55) |
|-------|-----------|--------|----------------------------------------------------------|
| `frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild` 0.60 | 0.60 | **0.27** | Sprint 57.43 actual 0.41 / Sprint 57.44 actual ~0.20 at 0.55 ظْ equivalent at 0.45 would be 0.34 / 0.16; still likely BELOW band ظ¤ flag for Sprint 57.46 retro evaluation |
| `frontend-verbatim-css-repoint -with-extras` 0.65 | 0.65 | **0.29** | Sprint 57.39 actual 0.41 at 0.55 ظْ equivalent at 0.45 ظëê 0.34; still likely BELOW band |
| `frontend-verbatim-css-repoint -simple` 0.50 | 0.50 | **0.225** | not yet validated under agent-delegation |
| `medium-frontend` 0.65 | 0.65 | **0.29** | not yet validated |

**Activation history under 0.55 (deprecated 2026-05-26)**: 2 data points 57.43=0.41 + 57.44=0.20 ظ¤ both BELOW band by 0.44 / 0.65 (mean ~0.305). Rollback rule "2 sprints with ratio < 0.7 ظْ tighten to 0.45" MET; structural decision Sprint 57.44 retro Q4. Residual speedup post-tightening predicted ~0.16-0.34 range (still significantly below band); next Sprint 57.45 retro will assess whether further tightening 0.45 ظْ 0.35 OR Option B per-class sub-class split is needed.

**Rollback rule** (3-sprint window ظ¤ parallel to existing `When to adjust the multiplier` discipline):
- If activated factor produces **2 sprints with `actual/committed-with-agent-factor` ratio < 0.7** ظْ tighten to `0.45`
- If activated factor produces **1 sprint with ratio > 1.20** ظْ roll back to `0.65` (single-data-point caution)
- If activated factor produces **ظëح 2 sprints with ratio > 1.20** ظْ roll back to `1.0` (drop the modifier ظ¤ agent delegation didn't actually accelerate; class-multiplier alone sufficient)

**Escalation to Option B** (per-class sub-class split ظ¤ fallback if Option A undershoots specific classes):
- If `0.55` produces ratio < 0.7 OR > 1.20 for **ظëح 2 specific classes** over 3-sprint window ظْ switch from Option A to Option B per-class split (add `+ agent-delegated` sub-row for each high-volume class; proposed baseline ranges: `-with-extras` 0.30-0.40 / `mockup-strict-rebuild` 0.25-0.35 / `verbatim-css-repoint -simple` 0.25-0.30; matches existing matrix granularity)

**Tracking discipline** (MANDATORY from Sprint 57.43+):

Each agent-delegated sprint MUST record in retrospective Q2:
1. `actual/bottom-up` ratio (existing)
2. `actual/committed` ratio (now `committed = bottom_up ├ù scope_class_mult ├ù agent_factor`)
3. **NEW**: explicit `agent-delegated: yes / no / partial` tag (ظëح 80% = `yes`; 20-79% = `partial`; < 20% = `no`)

Sprint plan ┬دWorkload Calibration MUST state estimate in the **four-segment form** when agent delegation is anticipated:

> Bottom-up est ~X hr ظْ class-calibrated commit ~Y hr (mult Z) ظْ agent-adjusted commit ~Y' hr (agent_factor 0.55)

where `Y' = Y ├ù 0.55 = X ├ù Z ├ù 0.55`. See ┬دWorkload Calibration ┬دFour-segment form above.

**Why this activation matters**: pre-activation, the matrix treated agent-delegated sprints as human-rewrite work, producing systematic ratio-below-band signals that looked like "calibration drift" when they were actually "missing agent_factor coefficient" (4 consecutive `mockup-strict-rebuild` ratios 0.36 / 0.18 / 0.33 + Sprint 57.39 `-with-extras` 0.41 all below band). Activating Option A correctly attributes the speedup AND resets the matrix to track real per-class calibration drift (independent of delegation-vs-human-cadence drift). Post-activation, the existing per-class multipliers stay UNCHANGED ظ¤ they remain calibrated to the human-rewrite cadence; `agent_factor` is a separate orthogonal coefficient applied on top.

**Note on `frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild` baseline lift proposal**: A separate carryover AD (`AD-Sprint-Plan-frontend-mockup-strict-rebuild-baseline-lift`) proposes lifting the `mockup-strict-rebuild` class multiplier from 0.60 ظْ 0.40-0.45. **This proposal is SUPERSEDED by `agent_factor = 0.55` activation**: the systematic below-band signal was the agent-delegation factor, not class-level calibration drift. KEEP 0.60 baseline for `mockup-strict-rebuild`; the new effective ratio under agent-delegation will be 0.60 ├ù 0.55 = 0.33 (matches Sprint 57.42 actual bullseye). If Sprint 57.43+ data points under combined `0.60 ├ù 0.55` still consistently undershoot, then class-level recalibration would be the next move per existing `When to adjust the multiplier` rule.
